[set FBD model]

	prset brlenspr=clock:fossilization;
	prset clockvarpr=igr;	
	prset igrvarpr=uniform(0.0001, 200) ; [an actual vague prior]
	prset clockratepr = normal(0.0025,1); [A very flat prior with same mean; although this will be truncated at 0, and true mean=0.82, it will be very very flat]
	prset nodeagepr = calibrated;
	prset speciationpr = uniform(0,10);
	prset extinctionpr = beta(0.5,0.5); [flat, extinction is relative to speciation thus between 0-1]
	prset fossilizationpr = beta(0.5,0.5); [flat, sampling is psi/(mu+psi), 0-1]
	prset samplestrat = random; [default: bdss prior]
	prset sampleprob = 0.000194; [NB % of extant taxa sampled; ~7/36,000]
	prset treeagepr = uniform (425, 458.18); [upper bound established by early 'ostracoderms']


[MCMC]

	[mcmc ngen=50000000 append=no;]

	mcmc ngen=6000000 relburnin=yes burninfrac=0.5 printfreq=5000 nruns=2 samplefreq=5000 nchains=4 savebrlens=yes temp=0.01;	
	
	sump;
	
	sumt contype=allcompat;

	end;
